349" y: b.samples,\n"
350" x: b.samples.map(function (_, i) { return i; })\n"
351" }\n"
352" });\n"
353" var layout = {\n"
354" title: data.title,\n"
355" showLegend: true,\n"
356" xaxis: { title: 'Measurement' },\n"
357" yaxis: {\n"
358" title: 'Time (' + data.units + ')',\n"
359" rangemode: 'tozero',\n"
360" zeroline: true\n"
361" },\n"
362" legend: legendStyle\n"
363" };\n"
364" Plotly.newPlot(plotdiv, traces, layout);\n"
365" }\n"
366"\n"
367" function plotSummary() {\n"
368" var traces = data.runs[0].benchmarks.map(function (b, i) {\n"
369" return {\n"
370" name: b.name,\n"
371" type: 'scatter',\n"
372" mode: 'markers',\n"
373" marker: { symbol: i },\n"
374" x: data.runs.map(function (r) { return r.params['LAYER']; }),\n"
375" y: data.runs.map(function (r) { return r.benchmarks[i].mean; }),\n"
376" }\n"
377" });\n"
378" var layout = {\n"
379" title: data.title,\n"
380" showLegend: true,\n"
381" xaxis: {\n"
382" title: 'Layer',\n"
383" tickmode: 'array',\n"
384" tickvals: data.runs.map(function (r) { return r.params['LAYER']; }),\n"
385" type: data.logarithmic ? 'log' : '',\n"
386" },\n"
387" yaxis: {\n"
388" title: 'Time (' + data.units + ')',\n"
389" rangemode: 'tozero',\n"
390" zeroline: true,\n"
391" type: data.logarithmic ? 'log' : '',\n"
392" },\n"
393" legend: legendStyle\n"
394" };\n"
395" Plotly.newPlot(plotdiv, traces, layout);\n"
396" }\n"
397"\n"
398" function plotSingleSummary() {\n"
399" var traces = data.runs[0].benchmarks.map(function (b, i) {\n"
400" return {\n"
401" type: 'bar',\n"
402" name: b.name,\n"

414" showLegend: true,\n"
415" xaxis: {\n"

417" showticklabels: false,\n"
418" },\n"
